HMP_sov_LL_monthly_effect = {
	ENG = {  
		# Reset monthly lend-lease variables
		clear_variable = SOV_ll_monthly_generation
		clear_variable = SOV_ll_this_month
		clear_variable = SOV_ll_monthly_cap

		# If Germany is at war with the Soviet Union
		if = {
			limit = { GER = { has_war_with = SOV } }

			# Murmansk / Archangelsk route
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							USA = { controls_state = 416 } # Iceland
							SOV = { controls_state = 408 } # Murmansk
						}
						has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_cap value = 5 }
			}

			# Persian corridor
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							ENG = { controls_state = 412 } # Iraq
							SOV = { controls_state = 412 }
						}
						SOV = { controls_state = 229 } # Persia
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 7 }
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_cap value = 25 }
			}

			# Vladivostok route
			if = {
				limit = { SOV = { controls_state = 213 } } # Vladivostok
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 3 }
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_cap value = 5 }
			}

			# Arctic convoy route
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						ENG = { controls_state = 116 } # Scotland
						SOV = { controls_state = 137 } # Archangelsk
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_cap value = 3 }
			}

			# Pacific route ‚Äď blocked unless USA controls or Japan excluded
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { JAP = { controls_state = 526 } } # Korea
						JAP = { is_subject_of = USA }
						has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { JAP = { controls_state = 560 } } # Taiwan
						JAP = { is_subject_of = USA }
						has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { JAP = { controls_state = 488 } } # Sakhalin
						JAP = { is_subject_of = USA }
						has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { JAP = { controls_state = 180 } } # Kurils
						JAP = { is_subject_of = USA }
						has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
			}

			# Convoys through Gibraltar & Suez if no western war
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = { controls_state = 336 } # Gibraltar
					NOT = { has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start }
					ENG = { controls_state = 326 } # Suez
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
			}

			# Japan blocking another route
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { JAP = { controls_state = 409 } } # Manchuria
						JAP = { is_subject_of = USA }
						has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 1 }
			}

			# USA special focuses increasing lend-lease
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_support_sov }
						has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start
						date > 1942.4.15
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_cap value = 10 }
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_secure_allied_shipping }
						has_global_flag = war_in_the_west_start
						date > 1942.4.15
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_cap value = 10 }
				add_to_variable = { var = SOV_ll_monthly_generation value = 10 }
			}
		}

		# Update monthly variables after routes are checked
		add_to_variable = { var = SOV_barb_ll_token value = SOV_ll_monthly_generation } 
		set_variable = { var = SOV_total_IC_sent value = SOV_barb_ll_token2 }
		multiply_variable = { var = SOV_total_IC_sent value = 2000 }
	}

	SWE = { 
		# Debug: sends insane test amounts (1,000,000 each)
		send_equipment = { equipment = infantry_equipment        amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #1
		send_equipment = { equipment = artillery_equipment       amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #2
		send_equipment = { equipment = anti_tank_equipment       amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #3	
		send_equipment = { equipment = support_equipment         amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #4
		send_equipment = { equipment = rocket_artillery_equipment amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #5
		send_equipment = { equipment = anti_air_equipment        amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #6

		send_equipment = { equipment = small_plane_airframe      amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #7 
		send_equipment = { equipment = small_plane_cas_airframe  amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #8
		send_equipment = { equipment = mech_chassis              amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #9
		send_equipment = { equipment = medium_tank_chassis       amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #10
		send_equipment = { equipment = light_tank_chassis        amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #11
		send_equipment = { equipment = motorized_equipment       amount = 1000000 target = SOV } #12
	}
}

# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ
# ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ

endsieg_production_buff_calc = {

	# Reset main variables and arrays
	clear_variable = GER.GER_engsieg_output 
	clear_array    = GER.ENDSIEG_SOV
	clear_array    = GER.ENDSIEG_BLK
	clear_array    = GER.ENDSIEG_ITA
	clear_array    = GER.ENDSIEG_FRA
	clear_array    = GER.ENDSIEG_GER

	# -------------------------------
	# Soviet states
	# -------------------------------
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			controller = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
			OR = {
				state = 228 state = 227 state = 200 state = 196 state = 137 state = 226 state = 197 state = 221 state = 259 state = 203 state = 240 state = 220 state = 225 state = 222 state = 223 state = 205 
				state = 242 state = 246 state = 263 state = 208 state = 224 state = 193 state = 243 state = 209 state = 13 state = 191 state = 12 state = 210 state = 190 state = 189 state = 11 state = 512 state = 96 
				state = 207 state = 241 state = 206 state = 95 state = 192 state = 287 state = 78 state = 198 state = 202 state = 199 state = 201 state = 194 state = 204 state = 94 state = 93 state = 91 state = 89 
				state = 80 state = 97 state = 245 state = 218 state = 234 state = 238 state = 217 state = 237 state = 235 state = 232 state = 233 state = 231 state = 230 state = 229 state = 236 state = 265 
				state = 260 state = 239 state = 258 state = 257 state = 254 state = 219 state = 247 state = 244 state = 264 state = 146 state = 216 state = 215 state = 213
			} # Soviet states
		}
		add_to_array = { array = GER.ENDSIEG_SOV value = THIS }
	}
	set_variable      = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_SOV value = GER.ENDSIEG_SOV^num }
	multiply_variable = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_SOV value = 0.005 }
	add_to_variable   = { var = GER.GER_engsieg_output value = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_SOV }
	clear_variable    = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_SOV
	
	# -------------------------------
	# Balkans + Norway + C. Europe (excluding GER)
	# -------------------------------
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			controller = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
			OR = {
				state = 186 state = 185 state = 47 state = 486 state = 44 state = 184 state = 106 state = 105 state = 212 state = 613 state = 48 state = 211 state = 293 state = 77 state = 46 state = 79 state = 108 state = 107 
				state = 414 state = 45 state = 104 state = 103 state = 109 state = 163 state = 81 state = 82 state = 84 state = 83 state = 76 state = 73 state = 154 state = 43 state = 155 state = 514 state = 303 state = 71  
				state = 578 state = 70 state = 102 state = 31 state = 22 state = 25 state = 33 state = 26 state = 20 state = 507 state = 314 state = 144 state = 143 state = 142 state = 110
			} # Balkans + Norway + Central Europe (non-GER)
		}
		add_to_array = { array = GER.ENDSIEG_BLK value = THIS }
	}
	set_variable      = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_BLK value = GER.ENDSIEG_BLK^num }
	multiply_variable = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_BLK value = 0.015 }
	add_to_variable   = { var = GER.GER_engsieg_output value = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_BLK }
	clear_variable    = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_BLK

	# -------------------------------
	# Italian states
	# -------------------------------
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			controller = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
			OR = {
				state = 115 state = 156 state = 117 state = 157 state = 2 state = 162 state = 161 state = 158 state = 313 state = 32 state = 21 state = 159 state = 39 state = 160
			} # Italy
		}
		add_to_array = { array = GER.ENDSIEG_ITA value = THIS }
	}
	set_variable      = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_ITA value = GER.ENDSIEG_ITA^num }
	multiply_variable = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_ITA value = 0.025 }
	add_to_variable   = { var = GER.GER_engsieg_output value = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_ITA }
	clear_variable    = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_ITA

	# -------------------------------
	# France + Low Countries + Denmark + Poland
	# -------------------------------
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			controller = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
			OR = {
				state = 19 state = 23 state = 30 state = 14 state = 15 state = 24 state = 27 state = 17 state = 18 state = 16 state = 267 state = 29 state = 34 state = 36 state = 7 state = 35 state = 6 state = 37 state = 99 
				state = 88 state = 72 state = 75 state = 9 state = 90 state = 92 state = 10 state = 87 state = 86 state = 98 state = 553
			} # France + Benelux + Denmark + Poland
		}
		add_to_array = { array = GER.ENDSIEG_FRA value = THIS }
	}
	set_variable      = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_FRA value = GER.ENDSIEG_FRA^num }
	multiply_variable = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_FRA value = 0.03 }
	add_to_variable   = { var = GER.GER_engsieg_output value = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_FRA }
	clear_variable    = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_FRA

	# -------------------------------
	# German core states
	# -------------------------------
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			controller = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
			OR = {
				state = 188 state = 330 state = 5 state = 556 state = 85 state = 63 state = 4 state = 152 state = 52 state = 153 state = 50 state = 28 state = 8 state = 42 state = 51 state = 55 state = 54 state = 53 state = 69 
				state = 74 state = 67 state = 66 state = 68 state = 62 state = 64 state = 61 state = 58 state = 59 state = 56 state = 57 state = 65 state = 60
			} # German cores
		}
		add_to_array = { array = GER.ENDSIEG_GER value = THIS }
	}
	set_variable      = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_GER value = GER.ENDSIEG_GER^num }
	multiply_variable = { var = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_GER value = 0.04 }
	add_to_variable   = { var = GER.GER_engsieg_output value = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_GER }
	clear_variable    = GER.TEMP_ENDSIEG_GER
			
	# -------------------------------
	# Special case: Bitter Peace / Soviet collapse
	# -------------------------------
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				SOV = { surrender_progress > 0.98 }
				has_global_flag = a_bitter_peace_fired
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { var = GER.GER_engsieg_output value = -1.2 }

		# Ensure value never goes below zero
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GER.GER_engsieg_output < 0 } }
			set_variable = { var = GER.GER_engsieg_output value = 0 }
		}
	}
}


# ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó
# ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ
# ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ
# ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ

startup_events = {
	# Countries that trigger countrystartup.101
	every_country = {
		limit = { 
			OR = { tag = SPR tag = HUN tag = CZE tag = ROM tag = BUL } 
		}
		country_event = { id = countrystartup.101 }
	}

	# Countries that trigger countrystartup.100
	every_country = {
		limit = { 
			OR = { tag = CAN tag = SAF tag = NZL tag = AST tag = NOR tag = GRE tag = POL tag = BRA tag = HOL } 
		}
		country_event = { id = countrystartup.100 }
	}

	# Major countries with unique startup events
	ENG = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.102 } }
	FRA = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.103 } }
	USA = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.104 } }
	SOV = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.105 } }
	RAJ = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.106 } }
	GER = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.107 } }
	ITA = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.108 } }
	JAP = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.109 } }
	FIN = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.110 } }
	EFR = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.111 } }
	YUG = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.113 } }
	MAN = { country_event = { id = countrystartup.114 } }

	# Italy-related scripted events
	SIA = { country_event = { id = italy.971 } }
	ROM = { country_event = { id = italy.969 } }
	#NZL = { country_event = { id = italy.970 } }
	MON = { country_event = { id = italy.968 } }
	SAF = { country_event = { id = italy.973 } }
}



finish_french_colony_focuses = {
	# If France controls state 539
	if = {
		limit = { FRA = { controls_state = 539 } }

		# Transfer various French colonies to France if not already controlled
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { FRA = { controls_state = 277 } } } 
			FRA = { transfer_state = 277 } 
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { FRA = { controls_state = 445 } } } 
			FRA = { transfer_state = 445 } 
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { FRA = { controls_state = 543 } } } 
			FRA = { transfer_state = 543 } 
		}
	}

	# If England controls states 291 and 454
	if = {
		limit = { 
			ENG = { controls_state = 291 }
			ENG = { controls_state = 454 }
		}

		# Transfer Syria/Levant states to France if not already controlled
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { FRA = { controls_state = 554 } } } 
			FRA = { 
				transfer_state = 589 
				transfer_state = 590 
				transfer_state = 591 
				transfer_state = 554 
			} 
		}
	}
}


copy_australian_at_equipment_research = {
	if = { limit = { AST = { has_tech = antitank2 }}  ROOT = { set_technology = { antitank2 = 1 }} }
	if = { limit = { AST = { has_tech = antitank5 }}  ROOT = { set_technology =  { antitank5 = 1 }} }
}

add_ruling_to_dem = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = add_ruling_to_dem_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = neutrality_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@neutrality
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = democratic_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@democratic
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = communism_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@communism
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = fascism_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@fascism
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				democratic_support_var = neutrality_support_var
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = neutrality_support_var
				value = 0
			}
		}

		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = neutrality_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@neutrality
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = democratic_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@democratic
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = communism_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@communism
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = fascism_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@fascism
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				democratic_support_var = communism_support_var
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = communism_support_var
				value = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = neutrality_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@neutrality
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = democratic_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@democratic
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = communism_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@communism
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = fascism_support_var
				value = party_popularity_100@fascism
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				democratic_support_var = fascism_support_var
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = fascism_support_var
				value = 0
			}
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = democratic_support_var
			neutrality = neutrality_support_var
			fascism = fascism_support_var
			communism = communism_support_var
		}
	}
}

# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ
# ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ

POL_april_constitution_up = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = POL_april_constitution_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = POL_april_constitution_1
			add_idea = POL_april_constitution_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = POL_april_constitution_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = POL_april_constitution_2
			add_idea = POL_april_constitution_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = POL_april_constitution_3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = POL_april_constitution_3
			add_idea = POL_april_constitution_4
		}
	}
}

POL_april_constitution_remove = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = POL_april_constitution_1
		}
		remove_ideas = POL_april_constitution_1
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = POL_april_constitution_2
		}
		remove_ideas = POL_april_constitution_2
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = POL_april_constitution_3
		}
		remove_ideas = POL_april_constitution_3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = POL_april_constitution_4
		}
		remove_ideas = POL_april_constitution_4
	}
}


# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ

ITA_bop_remove_lost_core_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_5
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_5
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_4
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_4
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_3
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_3
		}
	}
    if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_2
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_1
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_1
		}
	}
}



ITA_missiolinis_initialize_missiolinis_system = {
	set_country_flag = ITA_missiolinis_system_active_flag
}

ITA_missiolinis_manage_next_mission = {
	log = "Managing next Mussolini, please hang on. Tack!"

	#Check for pre-scripted vs randomized missions
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_number_of_missions_triggered = 5 } # WARNING: 5 is the number of pre-scripted missions. If more pre-scripted missions are added or removed, adjust this value
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_randomize_missiolinis_flag
	}

	if = { #PRE-SCRIPTED MISSIOLINIS
		limit = {
			NOT = {	has_country_flag = ITA_randomize_missiolinis_flag }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_number_of_missions_triggered = 1 } # WARNING: 5 is the number of pre-scripted missions. If more pre-scripted missions are added or removed, adjust this value
			}


			add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_number_of_missions_triggered = 1 }
		}


	}
	else = { #RANDOM MISSIOLINIS TIME

	}
}

ITA_missiolinis_initialize_new_mission_effect = { #Sets flags and everything necessary to keep track of ongoing missions, last time a mission was issued, etc.
	set_country_flag = { flag = ITA_missiolini_activated_recently_flag days = 30 } #WARNING THIS IS NOT SYNC WITH THE REST OF STUFF USING THE VAR ITA_missiolinis_min_cd_between_missions

	add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_active_missions = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_number_of_missions_triggered = 1 }
}

ITA_missiolinis_revert_new_mission_initialization_effect = { #For when player chooses to re-roll for a new mission
	clr_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_activated_recently_flag

	add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_active_missions = -1 }
	add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_number_of_missions_triggered = -1 }
}

ITA_missiolinis_finalize_mission_effect = { #Sets flags and everything necessary to end a mission and keep track of ongoing missions, etc.
	add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_active_missions = -1 }
	add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_number_of_missions_resolved = 1 }
}

ITA_missiolinis_add_to_successful_missions = {
	add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_successful_missions = 1 }
	career_profile_step_missiolini = yes
}

ITA_missiolinis_add_to_failed_missions = {
	add_to_variable = { ITA_missiolinis_failed_missions = 1 }
}

ITA_missiolinis_reroll_cost = {
	add_political_power = -25
	ITA_bop_very_low_decrease_effect = yes

	custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_missiolinis_reroll_tt
}

ITA_mussolinis_reroll_cleanup_if_necessary = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_missiolinis_rerolling_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_missiolinis_rerolling_flag
	}
}


### STRENGTHEN HEAVY INDUSTRY ###
ITA_missiolini_strengthen_heavy_industry_failure_effect = {
	add_political_power = -25
	add_stability = -0.03
}

ITA_missiolini_strengthen_heavy_industry_success_effect = {
	add_political_power = 50
	add_stability = 0.03
	
	add_timed_idea = {
		idea = ITA_strengthened_heavy_industry
		days = 365
	}
}

### STRENGTHEN THE ARMY ###
ITA_missiolini_strengthen_the_army_failure_effect = {
	add_political_power = -25
	add_war_support = -0.03
	add_timed_idea = {
		idea = ITA_disgruntlement_in_the_army
		days = 180
	}
}

ITA_missiolini_strengthen_the_army_success_effect = {
	army_experience = 50
	add_command_power = 25
	add_war_support = 0.03
	add_timed_idea = {
		idea = ITA_strengthened_the_army
		days = 365
	}
}

### STOCKPILE TRUCKS ###
ITA_missiolini_stockpile_trucks_failure_effect = {
	add_political_power = -25
	add_war_support = -0.03
}

ITA_missiolini_stockpile_trucks_success_effect = {
	if = { #DEFAULT
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = ITA_to_live_as_a_lion }
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ITA_efficient_supply_lines
			days = 365
		}
	}
	else = { # GREATER REWARD (from To Live as a Lion focus)
		add_political_power = 75
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ITA_efficient_supply_lines_lion_version
			days = 365
		}
	}
}

### INDUSTRIAL RESEARCH ###
ITA_missiolini_industrial_research_failure_effect = {
	add_political_power = -25
	add_popularity = {
		ideology = ROOT
		popularity = -0.05
	}

	#CLEAR FLAGS FOR NEXT TIME
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_production_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_production_flag
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_industry_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_industry_flag
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_construction_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_construction_flag
	}
}

ITA_missiolini_industrial_research_success_effect = {
	if = { #DEFAULT
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = ITA_to_live_as_a_lion }
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = ITA_missiolini_industrial_research
			bonus = 0.25
			uses = 2
			category = industry
			category = air_equipment
			category = naval_equipment
			category = artillery
			category = armor
			category = motorized_equipment
		}
	}
	else = { # GREATER REWARD (from To Live as a Lion focus)
		add_political_power = 35
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = ITA_missiolini_industrial_research
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 2
			category = industry
			category = air_equipment
			category = naval_equipment
			category = artillery
			category = armor
			category = motorized_equipment
		}
	}

	#CLEAR FLAGS FOR NEXT TIME
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_production_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_production_flag
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_industry_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_industry_flag
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_construction_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_missiolini_research_construction_flag
	}
}

		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = ROOT
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_timed_idea = { #First so that CP doesn't stack in case it's maxed out
			idea = ITA_bolstered_political_cabinet
			days = 365
		}
	}
	else = { # GREATER REWARD (from To Live as a Lion focus)
		add_political_power = 35
		add_command_power = 35
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = ROOT
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_timed_idea = { #First so that CP doesn't stack in case it's maxed out

			days = 365
		}
	}

# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ē¶‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ē¶‚ēĚ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ
# ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ

ITA_initiate_balance_of_power_effect = {
	set_power_balance = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		left_side = ITA_grand_council_side # will keep the last set side if not specified
		right_side = ITA_mussolini_side # will keep the last set side if not specified
		set_default = yes # whether or not to reset the power balance to the initial value, default = no
		#set_value = 0.25 # if specified will set the value of the power balance, this option will override the effect of set_default so the two options should not be used together. if neither set_default or set_value is specified the current value of the power balance will not change
	}
}

ITA_bop_absurdly_high_increase_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = 1
	}
}

ITA_bop_very_high_increase_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = 0.25
	}
}

ITA_bop_high_increase_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = 0.2
	}
}

ITA_bop_medium_increase_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = 0.15
	}
}

ITA_bop_low_increase_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = 0.1
	}
}

ITA_bop_very_low_increase_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = 0.05
	}
}

ITA_bop_absurdly_high_decrease_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = -1
	}
}

ITA_bop_very_high_decrease_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = -0.25
	}
}

ITA_bop_high_decrease_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = -0.2
	}
}

ITA_bop_medium_decrease_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = -0.15
	}
}

ITA_bop_low_decrease_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = -0.1
	}
}

ITA_bop_very_low_decrease_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = -0.05
	}
}

ITA_bop_increase_lost_core_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_4
			}
		}
		add_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_3
			}
		}
		add_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_2
			}
		}
		add_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_1
			}
		}
		add_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_power_balance_modifier = {
					id = ITA_power_balance
					modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_5
				}
			}
		}
		add_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_1
		}
	}
}

ITA_bop_decrease_lost_core_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_5
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_4
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_3
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_2
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = ITA_power_balance
				modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_1
			}
		}
		remove_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = ITA_power_balance
			modifier = ITA_power_balance_lost_core_1
		}
	}
	else = {
		#NOTHING cannot decrease
	}
}

ITA_bop_remove_bop_effect = {
	remove_power_balance = { id = ITA_power_balance }
}

ITA_remove_king_vittorio_emanuele_as_idea = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = vittorio_emanuele
		}
		remove_ideas = vittorio_emanuele
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = vittorio_emanuele_king_of_albania
		}
		remove_ideas = vittorio_emanuele_king_of_albania
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = vittorio_emanuele_emperor_of_ethiopia
		}
		remove_ideas = vittorio_emanuele_emperor_of_ethiopia
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = vittorio_emanuele_albania_ethiopia
		}
		remove_ideas = vittorio_emanuele_albania_ethiopia
	}
}

ITA_add_king_vittorio_emanuele_back_as_idea = { #After having removed him
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = ITA_the_new_emperor_of_ethiopia
			ITA_vittorio_emanuele_iii = { has_character_flag = ITA_king_of_albania_flag }
		}
		add_ideas = vittorio_emanuele_albania_ethiopia

	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			ITA_vittorio_emanuele_iii = { has_character_flag = ITA_king_of_albania_flag }
		}
		add_ideas = vittorio_emanuele_king_of_albania
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = ITA_the_new_emperor_of_ethiopia
		}
		add_ideas = vittorio_emanuele_emperor_of_ethiopia
	}
	else = {
		add_ideas = vittorio_emanuele
	}
}

ITA_improve_regio_esercito_dm_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_dynamic_modifier }
			# Fake update to get the other ones in the correct place
			# Airforce
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			# Navy
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_3_dynamic_modifier }
			# Fake update to get the other ones in the correct place
			# Airforce
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			# Navy
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_alt_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			# Fake update to get the other ones in the correct place
			# Airforce
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			# Navy
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {

				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }

			}

					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}

	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_alt_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {

			}
			else_if = {

				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }

ITA_improve_regia_aeronautica_dm_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
			# Fake update to get the other ones in the correct place
			# Airforce
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
			# Fake update to get the other ones in the correct place
			# Airforce
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_alt_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			# Fake update to get the other ones in the correct place
			# Airforce
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			# Fake update to get the other ones in the correct place
			# Airforce
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}

ITA_improve_regia_marina_dm_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier	}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
		}
	}
}

#Change name of States and VPs when appropriate. Expected to be used inside on_state_control_changed. FROM.FROM is state / ROOT is new controller / FROM is former controller
ITA_change_name_of_state_or_vp = {
	if = { # Fiume / Rijeka
		limit = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				state = 852 #ISTRIA
			}
		}
		if = { #ITALY CONTROLLER
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = ITA }
			}
			set_province_name = { id = 11564 name = VICTORY_POINTS_11564_ITA }
		}
		else_if = { #OTHER CONTROLLER
			limit = {
				FROM = { original_tag = ITA }
			}
			reset_province_name = 11564
		}
	}
	else_if = { # ZARA / ZADAR // Zara / Zadar
		limit = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				state = 163 #ZARA
			}
		}
		if = { #ITALY CONTROLLER
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = ITA }
			}
			FROM.FROM = { set_state_name = STATE_163_ITA }
			set_province_name = { id = 3943 name = VICTORY_POINTS_3943_ITA }
		}
		else_if = { #OTHER CONTROLLER
			limit = {
				FROM = { original_tag = ITA }
			}
			FROM.FROM = { reset_state_name = yes }
			reset_province_name = 3943
		}
	}
	else_if = { # DODECANESO / DODECANESE // Rodi / Rhodes
		limit = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				state = 164 #DODECANESO
			}
		}
		if = { #ITALY CONTROLLER
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = ITA }
			}
			FROM.FROM = { set_state_name = VICTORY_POINTS_10007_ITA }
			set_province_name = { id = 10007 name = VICTORY_POINTS_10007_ITA }
		}
		else_if = { #OTHER CONTROLLER
			limit = {
				FROM = { original_tag = ITA }
			}
			FROM.FROM = { reset_state_name = yes }
			reset_province_name = 10007
		}
	}
}

ITA_replace_stuff_based_on_ideology_effect = {
	ROOT = {
		if = { # No king
			limit = {
				ITA_has_rejected_monarchy = yes
			}
			# REGIO ESERCITO
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}

			# REGIA AERONAUTICA
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}

			# REGIA AERONAUTICA
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
			}
		}
		else = { #KING
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regio_esercito_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}

			# REGIA AERONAUTICA
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_aeronautica_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}

			# REGIA AERONAUTICA
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_2_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			else_if = {

				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_alt_dynamic_modifier }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_regia_marina_3_dynamic_modifier }
			}
		}
	}
}

# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ
# ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ÄÉ‚ÄÉ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ

ITA_bop_absurdly_high_increase_balbo_side_effect = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = 1
		tooltip_side = ITA_balbo_side
	}
}

	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = ITA_power_balance
		value = 0.25
		tooltip_side = ITA_balbo_side
	}
}

		value = 0.2
		tooltip_side = ITA_balbo_side
	}
}

	}

ITA_create_edgardo_sogno_operative = { #DEMOCRATIC (Liberal)
	create_operative_leader = {
		name = "Edgardo Sogno"
		GFX = GFX_portrait_ITA_edgardo_sogno
		traits = { operative_linguist operative_natural_orator }
		bypass_recruitment = no
		available_to_spy_master = yes
		nationalities = { ITA }
	}
}


ITA_characters_to_purge_effect = {
	#ADVISORS
	if = {#First alternative for purge
		limit = {
			has_character = ITA_achille_starace
			ITA_achille_starace = { has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged }
		}
		ITA_achille_starace = { set_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor }
	}
	else_if = {#Second alternative if the first one isn't available
		limit = {
			has_character = ITA_carlo_scorza
			ITA_carlo_scorza = { has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged }
		}
		ITA_carlo_scorza = { set_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor }
	}
	else = {#Third, random alternative if the first two aren't available
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged
				is_character_slot = political_advisor
			}
			set_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor
		}
	}
	if = {#First alternative for purge
		limit = {
			has_character = ITA_renato_ricci
			ITA_renato_ricci = { has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged }
		}
		ITA_renato_ricci = { set_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor }
	}
	else_if = {#Second alternative if the first one isn't available
		limit = {
			has_character = ITA_roberto_farinacci
			ITA_roberto_farinacci = { has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged }
		}
		ITA_roberto_farinacci = { set_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor }
	}
	else = {#Third, random alternative if the first two aren't available
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged
				is_character_slot = political_advisor
				NOT = { has_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor }
			}
			set_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor
		}
	}
	#GENERALS
	if = {#First alternative for purge
		limit = {
			has_character = ITA_rodolfo_graziani
			ITA_rodolfo_graziani = { has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged }
		}
		ITA_rodolfo_graziani = { set_character_flag = ITA_purge_general }
	}
	else_if = {#Second alternative if the first one isn't available
		limit = {
			has_character = ITA_ugo_cavallero
			ITA_ugo_cavallero = { has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged }
		}
		ITA_ugo_cavallero = { set_character_flag = ITA_purge_general }
	}
	else = {#Third, random alternative if the first two aren't available
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged
				is_unit_leader = yes
			}
			set_character_flag = ITA_purge_general
		}
	}
	if = {#First alternative for purge
		limit = {
			has_character = ITA_ubaldo_soddu
			ITA_ubaldo_soddu = { has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged }
		}
		ITA_ubaldo_soddu = { set_character_flag = ITA_purge_general }
	}
	else_if = {#Second alternative if the first one isn't available
		limit = {
			has_character = ITA_francesco_zingales
			ITA_francesco_zingales = { has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged }
		}
		ITA_francesco_zingales = { set_character_flag = ITA_purge_general }
	}
	else = {#Third, random alternative if the first two aren't available
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged
				is_unit_leader = yes
				NOT = { has_character_flag = ITA_purge_general }
			}
			set_character_flag = ITA_purge_general
		}
	}
}

#Retire characters with the flag from the game OR remove the flag but keep the character
ITA_purge_advisors_effect = {
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor
		}
		retire = yes
	}
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = ITA_purge_general
		}
		clr_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged
	}
}

#Retire characters with the flag from the game OR remove the flag but keep the character
ITA_purge_generals_effect = {
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor
		}
		clr_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged
	}
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = ITA_purge_general
		}
		retire = yes
	}
}

#Removes the purge flag from characters that was spared the purge
ITA_dont_purge_effect = {
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor
		}

		clr_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged
		clr_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor
	}
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = ITA_purge_general
		}

		clr_character_flag = ITA_character_can_be_purged
		clr_character_flag = ITA_purge_general
	}
}

#Removes purge flags
ITA_clear_purge_flag_effect = {
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor
		}

		clr_character_flag = ITA_purge_advisor
	}
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = ITA_purge_general
		}

		clr_character_flag = ITA_purge_general
	}
}




# ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ
# ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ
# ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ
# ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ

# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēó‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēź‚ēź‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĒ‚ēĚ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚Ėą‚Ėą‚ēĎ
# ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ‚ĖĎ‚ĖĎ‚ēö‚ēź‚ēĚ

SOV_achievement_propaganda_counter_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = propaganda_counter value = 1 compare = less_than }
		}
		set_variable = { var = propaganda_counter value = 1 } #setup variable
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = {
			propaganda_counter = 1
		}
	}
}
SOV_pick_propaganda_campaign_slot_effect = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_left_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_left_icon_frame = SOV_new_propaganda_campaign }
			#Ageing posters
			set_variable = { SOV_propaganda_left_poster_to_age = SOV_poster_left_icon_frame } #This is used to prevent the system to break if a propaganda campaign is cancelled
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = NSB_soviet_propaganda_capmaign_events.101 days = SOV_default_propaganda_campaign_old_days }
				#set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_left_days_remaining_flag days = SOV_default_propaganda_campaign_duration } #Surprise! This doesn√§t work with vars :D  Maybe in the future
				if = { #Debug -> Faster time
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = SOV_debug_fast_propaganda_campaigns_flag
					}
					set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_left_days_remaining_flag days = 5 }
				}
				else = { #Regular time
					set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_left_days_remaining_flag days = 180 } #Need code support to use a var here
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_center_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_center_icon_frame = SOV_new_propaganda_campaign }
			#Ageing posters
			set_variable = { SOV_propaganda_center_poster_to_age = SOV_poster_center_icon_frame } #This is used to prevent the system to break if a propaganda campaign is cancelled
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = NSB_soviet_propaganda_capmaign_events.102 days = SOV_default_propaganda_campaign_old_days }
				#set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_center_days_remaining_flag days = SOV_default_propaganda_campaign_duration } #Surprise! This doesn√§t work with vars :D  Maybe in the future
				if = { #Debug -> Faster time
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = SOV_debug_fast_propaganda_campaigns_flag
					}
					set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_center_days_remaining_flag days = 5 }
				}
				else = { #Regular time
					set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_center_days_remaining_flag days = 180 } #Need code support to use a var here
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_right_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_right_icon_frame = SOV_new_propaganda_campaign }
			#Ageing posters
			set_variable = { SOV_propaganda_right_poster_to_age = SOV_poster_right_icon_frame } #This is used to prevent the system to break if a propaganda campaign is cancelled
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = NSB_soviet_propaganda_capmaign_events.103 days = SOV_default_propaganda_campaign_old_days }
				#set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_right_days_remaining_flag days = SOV_default_propaganda_campaign_duration } #Surprise! This doesn√§t work with vars :D  Maybe in the future
				if = { #Debug -> Faster time
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = SOV_debug_fast_propaganda_campaigns_flag
					}
					set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_right_days_remaining_flag days = 5 }
				}
				else = { #Regular time
					set_country_flag = { flag = SOV_propaganda_right_days_remaining_flag days = 180 } #Need code support to use a var here
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { SOV_new_propaganda_campaign = 0 } # Reset var
		add_to_variable = { SOV_propaganda_campaigns_taken = 1 } #Update propaganda campaigns counter
	}
}

SOV_reset_propaganda_campaign_slot_effect = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_left_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_campaign_to_remove }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_left_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
			#Clear aged posters
			clear_variable = SOV_propaganda_left_poster_to_age
			clr_country_flag = SOV_propaganda_left_slot_is_old_flag
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_center_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_campaign_to_remove }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_center_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
			#Clear aged posters
			clear_variable = SOV_propaganda_center_poster_to_age
			clr_country_flag = SOV_propaganda_center_slot_is_old_flag
		}
		else_if = { #This could be turned into an else, but leaving it like this to hopefully make it easier to see
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_right_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_campaign_to_remove }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_right_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
			#Clear aged posters
			clear_variable = SOV_propaganda_right_poster_to_age
			clr_country_flag = SOV_propaganda_right_slot_is_old_flag
		}
		set_variable = { SOV_propaganda_campaign_to_remove = 0 } # Reset var
	}
}

SOV_unlock_propaganda_campaign_slot_effect = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_left_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_locked_slot_index }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_left_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_center_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_locked_slot_index }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_center_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_right_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
		}
	}
}

SOV_increase_propaganda_campaign_cost_effect = {
	multiply_variable = { SOV_propaganda_cost = SOV_propaganda_cost_increase } #Using generic var SOV_propaganda_cost so that we only need to change this operation to tweak all propagandas' cost escalation
}


# Gives a secret army modifier to the states that affect Soviet Lend-Lease

enable_ll = {
    # Apply dynamic modifiers to states receiving lend-lease
    every_state = {
        limit = { lend_lease_states_1 = yes }
        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = gabon_1 scope = SOV days = 150 }
    }

    every_state = {
        limit = { lend_lease_states_2 = yes }
        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = gabon_2 scope = SOV days = 150 }
    }
}



####
#### INDUSTRIAL STUFF ####
####

SOV_replace_industrial_designer = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_upgrade_industrial_designer_tt
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = stalingrad_tractor_factory
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = stalingrad_tractor_factory
			add_idea = stalingrad_tractor_factory_improved
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = leningrad_polytechnical_institute
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = leningrad_polytechnical_institute
			add_idea = leningrad_polytechnical_institute_improved
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_soviet_railways
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_soviet_railways
			add_idea = SOV_soviet_railways_improved
		}
	}
}



####
#### FOREIGN POLITICS ####
